It's a slightly cooler evening than the last couple of nights and we're on a new strip, with the square boundaries measuring 63m and 72m. The breeze is blowing across the ground towards the longer side, which should even things out. Busy traffic coming out of Rodney Bay and the ticket sales look good: there is still availability for premium seats but most of the stands and the grass banks have sold out." His <a href="https://www.espncricinfo.com/story/t20-world-cup-wi-vs-afg-time-for-johnson-charles-to-put-on-a-show-1439101">new story on Johnson Charles</a> also reminded me that West Indies coach Daren Sammy will be coaching his team at a stadium named for him today. <strong>7.30pm</strong> Hello and welcome to the last game of the group stages at the 2024 T20 World Cup. However, this series will provide opportunities to many in and around the squad to get familiar with the conditions and maybe make a statement after a break in their international-cricket calendar.
